08/06/20, 20:13 - Anuj Gupta: Write about the following topic:

The average standard of people's health is likely to be lower in the future than it is now.

To what extent do you agree or disagree with this statement?

Give reasons for your answer and include any relevant examples from your own knowledge or experience.
08/06/20, 20:13 - Anuj Gupta: I  would strongly disagree with this statement. We realise that definitely, today's youth is tending to live its life their own way and they somehow, have a strong disconnect with the traditional practices which are being followed world over. They donot stick to a healthy lifestyle and donot have a healthy diet. However, they are still more health conscious. They have a strong eye on the health parameters and if someone has a health issue, he or she is more prompt to approach a doctor. The people in today's time donot follow the instructions given to them by their elders in the family immediately and their counter these advises. However, they apply their intelligence, logics and then do research on the problems and then take action. Today's youth is more prompt in approaching diagnostic centers and get their tests done without doctor's advise. They would rather take the report to the doctor and then seek a treatment. You know why? They are more confident about themselves rather than listening to elders and believing the God that everything will be alright. They trust their actions and not beliefs of others. Knowledge is a bliss. Trust is a power. Absence of one of these lead to problems. Today's youth is full of these and tend to grow continuously on these fronts. Earlier , people used to have more fears about health and they used to stick to particular life styles, but they never analysed the causes of health problems when these occurred. They just put tot the God to take care of them. Some problems were cured by doctors, some went on their own and remaining, they had to face the consequences. So, all these reasons imply that average standard of the health will be better in the future than it is now.

I would cite a live example from my life. My son was diagnosed recently with a kidney stone. He suffered huge pains and we were literally helpless. We could not go out to doctors due to Corona fears. We tried various things viz. giving homeopathic medicines, excessive water for drinking etc. , but nothing worked. Then took medication from a Urologist and that did the things. Now, when we finally analysed the entire sequence of events, we realised that our son suffered from this because of this attitude. He never drank plenty of water. Whenever, we told him to do so, he ignored. We blamed him all the time for his habits.

Then he asked me a question as to why I could not guide him properly to follow a healthy lifestyle. He could drink water only when he felt need for it. He suffered from pain but he had the capacity to bear it and developed a faith in himself that he would be alright soon. He took medicines and continued to spend his time thinking that things would be alright. Also, he studied about the stones in this time on internet and figured out various things which could help him in future to avoid their re-occurrence. All it was about his trust and faith in his knowledge which he gained during this crisis. HE emerged stronger as a person. Instead of cursing God and his habits, he analysed the sequences and devised strategies to live his life in a more healthy way.

14/06/20, 11:47 - Mommy: Covid Medical kit Required at home:

1. Paracetamol
2. Betadine for mouthwash and gargle
3. Vitamin C and D3 
5. B complex 
6. Vapour+ capsules for steam
7. Oximeter 
8. Oxygen cylinder (for emergency only)
9. arogya Setu app 
10.Breathing Exercises 

Covid Three stages:

1. Covid only in nose - recovery  time is half a day. (Steam inhaling), vitamin C. Usually no fever. Asymptomatic. 

2. Covid in throat - sore throat, recovery time 1 day (hot water gargle, warm water to drink, if temp then paracetamol. Vitamin C, Bcomplex. If severe than antibiotic. 

3. Covid in lungs- coughing and breathlessness 4 to 5 days. (Vitamin C, B complex, hot water gargle, oximeter, paracetamol, cylinder if severe, lot of liquid required, deep breathing exercise.

Stage when to approach hospital:
Monitor the oxygen level. If it goes near 43 (normal 98-100) then you need oxygen cylinder. If available at home, then no hospital else admit.

07/07/20, 16:23 - Mommy: An engineer in a car manufacturing company designs a world class car. The CEO is impressed with the outcome and praised him a lot. 

While trying to bring out the car from the manufacturing area to the showroom, they realised that the car is 2 inches taller than the entrance.

The engineer felt bad that he didn't notice this one before creating the car.

The CEO was confused on how to take it outside of the manufacturing area.

The painter said that they can bring out the car and there will be a few scratches on top of the car which could be touched up later on.

The engineer said that they can break the entrance, take the car out, and later re-do it.

The CEO was not convinced with any ideas and felt like it is a bad sign to break or scratch. 

A Watchman was observing all the drama & slowly approached the CEO.  He wanted to give an idea if they had no problem. 

They wondered what this guy would tell them that the experts could not give.

The watchman said "The car is only a few inches taller than the entrance so, simply release the air in the tyre, the height of the car will sink and can be easily taken out"...

Everyone clapped!!!

Don't analyse the problems only from an expert point of view alone.

Life issues are also the same....

Think Simple...
Do Simple and Live Simple

Release some Air... It could be our 'anger' .... our 'disappointments'... our  'egos'... Our 'confusions' ..

1. Nokia refused Android

3. Kodak refused digital cameras 

Lessons:

1. Take risks
2. Embrace change
3. If you refuse to change with time, you will be obsoleted 

Two more stories:

1. Facebook takes over WhatsApp and Instagram
2. Grab takes over Uber in South East Asia

Lessons:

1. Become so powerful that your competitors become your allies
2. Reach the top position and then eliminate the competition
3. Keep innovating

Two more stories:

1. Colonel Sanders founded KFC at the age of 65
2. Jack Ma, who couldn't get a job at KFC, founded Alibaba, and retired at 55 

Lessons:

1. Age is just a number
2. Only those who keep trying will succeed

Lamborghini was founded as a result of the revenge of a tractor owner who was insulted by Enzo Ferrari, the founder of Ferrari

09/08/20, 18:11 - Mommy: Today , I went to the supermarket with the prudence dictated by the new normal. Mask, gel and safety distance. I then started to get the things that were on my short list, and when I was lining up to pay, between taking the money and storing the phone, the 500 rupees note I had to pay fell on the floor, and the man who was in front of me finishing paying his purchases slowly bent down and picked up my note.

Woww.. How much education and kindness in these pandemic times - I thought. I held out my hand, waiting for him to give me back my money, trying to stay away, so that he would feel safe, while preparing to thank him for the gesture.
But suddenly, what he told me was  shocking - What's on the floor belongs to whoever finds it! - and just like that, he left ... naturally, as if he hadn't done anything wrong.

I looked at the lady behind me and the people next to me and they all looked at me in shock and disbelief, whispering things between them.

For a moment there, I was trying to evaluate myself. I wanted to do justice on my own ... I left my purchases, because I had no way to pay, and went after him to the parking lot, to have my 500/- returned. What a THUG!!!!
However, I realized that the people closest to the line came after me, curious to know what was going to happen ...

I spoke to him ...demanding my money but he just looked at me with contempt and acted like I was invisible.

When he got to the car, he slowly put his two shopping bags on the floor to take the key out of his pocket and open the trunk, and I thought - It's now or never!
I took the two bags and told him the same thing he had said to me - "What is on the floor belongs to those who find it! " .......- and I started running towards the exit, between fright and laughter, proud of my revenge.

The spectators started to applaud and I saw that the “smart guy” had been irritated after all, as he left the parking lot dropping security cones in his path.
I swear I felt a rush of adrenaline, fright and nervousness, but then I cried with laughter.
When I got home I opened the bags and found:

- 2 kg apples
- 1 kg of sugar
-  cheese and yogurt of two flavors
- whole grain bread,
-  2 packs of orange juice
- 2 jars of strawberry jam
- 2 kg of very good quality green peas
- 1 jar of mayonnaise, HORLICKS, CHYAWANPRAASH
- 1KG LIQUID SUEF EXCEL
I had never made so many purchases with only 500 rupees
And now here I am ... Having a glass of orange juice, eating and thinking as I write - am I a vigilante or a vindictive person?

नवाब साहब को ये बहुत नागवार गुज़रा और उन्होंने कोर्ट में केस कर दिया। जज ने गधा बोलने वाले से पूछा तो उसने अपनी ग़लती मानते हुए माफ़ी माँग ली।

जज ने नवाब साहब से कहाः *"नवाब साहब अब तो ये माफ़ी माँग रहा है, आपका क्या कहना है?"*

इस पर नवाब साहब माफ़ी देने के लिये तैयार हो गये -- लेकिन शर्त रखी कि वह आदमी अब कभी किसी नवाब को गधा नहीं बोलेगा।

वो आदमी मान गया कि अब किसी नवाब को वो गधा नहीं बोलेगा।

जज ने मुजरिम को बरी कर दिया।

जाने से पहले उस आदमी ने जज साहब से पूछाः *"योर हॉनर, मैं नवाब साहब को तो कत्तई गधा नहीं बोलूंगा लेकिन एक बात बताइये कि गधे को तो मैं नवाब साहब बोल सकता हूँ कि नहीं?"*

जज ने कहा: *"गधे को आप कुछ भी बोलिए, कोर्ट का उससे कोई लेना देना नहीं है।"*

वो आदमी नवाब साहब की तरफ मुड़ा और बोलाः *अच्छा "नवाब साहब" चलता हूँ!"*

18/11/20, 20:53 - Mommy: Covid

  1. We may have to live with C19 for months or years.  Don't deny or panic.  Don't make your life a misery.  Let's learn to live with this reality.

  2. You can't destroy the C19 virus that has penetrated the cell walls, by drinking liters of hot water - you'll just be going to the bathroom more often.

  3. Washing your hands and maintaining a physical distance  is your best method of protection.

  4. If you do not have a C19 patient at home, there is no need to disinfect your home.

  5. Grocery bags / plastic bags, gas stations, shopping carts and ATMs do not cause infection.Wash your hands, live your life as usual.

  6. C19 is not a food infection.  It is associated with infectious droplets such as flu.  There is no demonstrated risk that C19 is transmitted by ordering food.

  7. You can lose your sense of smell by using a lot of anti-allergies and viral infections.  These are only non-specific symptoms of C19.

  8. Once you get home, you don't need to change clothes immediately and take a shower!
 Cleanliness is a virtue but not paranoia!

  9. The C19 virus does not fly through the air.  This is a respiratory drop infection that requires close contact.

  10.The air is clean, you can walk to parks and public places (just keep your physical distance for protection)

  11. Just use regular soap against C19, no need for anti-bacterial soap.  These are viruses, not bacteria.

  12. You don't have to worry about your food orders.  But you can heat everything in the microwave, if you want.

  13. The possibility of bringing the C19 home in your shoes is like being struck by lightning twice a day.  I've worked against viruses for 20 years - drop infections don't spread like that!

  14. You can't be protected from viruses by consuming vinegar, sugarcane juice and ginger!  It's just for immunity not medicine.

  15. Wearing a mask for a long time interferes with your breathing and oxygen levels.  Wear it only in crowded places.

  16. Wearing gloves is also a bad idea;  the virus can accumulate in gloves and is easily transmitted if you touch your face.  Better to just wash your hands regularly.

  17. Immune system gets very weak by always living in a sterile environment.  Even if we are taking immune-boosting supplements / medicines, please regularly leave your house to the park / beach or anywhere else.

12/02/21, 13:04 - Anuj Gupta: *When you have nothing better to do*
*Just try answers for these*

 1. If poison expires; is it more poisonous or is it no longer poisonous?
🤔
2. Which letter is silent in the word "Scent," the S or the C?
🤔
3. Do twins ever realize that one of them is "Unplanned"?
🤔
4. Why is the letter W, in English, called double U? Shouldn't it be called double V?
🤔
5. Maybe Oxygen is slowly killing you and It just takes 75-100 years to fully work.
🤔
6. Every time you clean something, you just make something else dirty.
🤔
7. The word "swims" upside-down is still "swims"
🤔
8. 100 years ago everyone owned a Horse and only the rich had Cars. Today everyone has Cars and only the rich own Horses.
🤔
9. If you replace "W" with "T" in "What, Where and When", you get the answer to each of them.
🤔
*Still have time for fun..?*
*Let's try this*

Six Great Confusions
Which are still unresolved
😄😂
1. At a movie theatre, which arm rest is yours?

2. If people evolve from monkeys, why are monkeys still around?

3. Why is there a 'D' in fridge,
but not in refrigerator?

4.  Who knew what time it was when the first clock was made?

*Well Try this now*
Vagaries of English Language! Enjoy.!!!
😀

•Wonder why the word "Funeral" starts with FUN?

•Why isn't a Fireman called a Water-man?

•How come Lipstick doesn't do what it says?

•If money doesn't grow on trees, how come Banks have Branches?

•If a Vegetarian eats vegetables, what does a Humanitarian eat?

•How do you get off a non-stop Flight?

•Why are goods sent by *Ship* called CARGO, and those sent by *Truck* SHIPMENT?

•Why do we put cups in the "Dishwasher" and the dishes in the "Cupboard"?

•Why do doctors "Practice" medicine? Are they having practice at the cost of the patients?

•Why is it called "Rush Hour" when traffic moves at its slowest then?

•How come Noses run and Feet smell?

•Why do they call it a TV 'set' when there is only one?

•What are you vacating when you go on a "Vacation"?

We can never find the answers
Can we❓

If you have the *Spirit* of understanding everything in a positive manner - You’ll enjoy every moment in LIFE, whether it’s *PRESSURE or PLEASURE*

So just enjoy the PUN and FUN of the English language.
😂🤣😂
Enjoy n have fun.😘👍

18/02/21, 00:31 - Anuj Gupta: Srishti's Assignment
18/02/21, 00:31 - Anuj Gupta: Q1. What are values? How important are they in your life?

Humans are social beings. They have feelings, emotions and their ways of living life. Values refer to our ethics which mean our perceptions driven by our core inner conscience which tells us as to what is right for us in terms of actions and reactions. Values play an integral part in our life. Without values, we are just living creatures who breathe, eat and do things to live life but we tend to live as if we have never lived life as a human , just a living creature. We need values to keep our self esteem high, equip ourselves with a sense of responsibilities, build relationships and live them with love, affection and dedication. Our values drive us to understand and perform our roles towards our family, society, country and humanity.

Q2. What values do you stand by / believe in?

Be a good human who knows his/ her duties. Best formula of life is to live peacefully and let others live peacefully. Do your best, don't hurt anyone, give love to all, help others to the best of your capability and above all, don't expect, just do your actions but in the right spirit of doing good with a sense of responsibility.

Q3. What changes would you like to see in yourself in the next one year?

Become more mature, focused and develop an understanding of what I aim to be in life.

Q4. List some of the changes you would like to see in your country in the next three years?

First of all, fight the pandemic of Covid and overcome this to live a normal life. Next, we need to control increasing prices. Improve discipline.

Q5. Do you know any person / people / institutions who are trying to bring about a positive change?

There is a famous saying - Charity begins at home. So first is myself and then my family - Parents and brother.

Q6. What problems do you foresee in achieving your goal?

Only one thing - Perseverance. This needs to stay. This is something which people lose. I wouldn't want to lose it.

Q7. How would you like to contribute to the betterment of your nation?

Become a responsible citizen. Excel in whatever I do and help people to live their lives better. Develop the sense of responsibility amongst others whom I can influence. Whoever I meet, I aim to tell them one thing - become a good human first. then you can become a better professional.

23/03/21, 00:29 - Anuj Gupta: Some details about ETO
23/03/21, 00:35 - Anuj Gupta: 1. ETO Electric Mobility is a full-fledged *Electric Mobility Solutions & Services Company* that provides mobility solutions for both passenger and cargo segments.

2. ETO also offers e-rickshaws and e-autos on a daily rental basis in both passenger and cargo segments for its Driver Partners to earn their livelihood.

3. 2400 vehicles Fleet

4. Operation in 10 cities

5. As an EV fleet company ETO will take care of charging, maintenance, and overnight parking costs.

6. It offers *Corporate fleet solutions.*

7. Last Mile connectivity solutions with Metro corporations.

8. 300 Electric autos given to Big-basket for delivery operations (made by Keto motors).

9. Takes a fleet of vehicles from Keto Motors (wholly owned subsidiary of ETO), Goenka Electric Motors.

11. ETO has a stake in Goenka Electric.

12. ETO has a Memorandum of Understanding (MoU) with the Telangana government to set up a greenfield manufacturing facility for its range of electric vehicles, including three wheelers. The manufacturing unit will be set up under its subsidiary Keto Motors, with an investment of Rs 150 crore.

13. They tied up with Zoomcar to provide Last Mile connectivity on Jamia Metro owning the fleet.

14. The consortium led by ETO Motors along with its partner Goenka Electric Motor Vehicles has received the Expression of Interest (EOI) by the Delhi Metro Rail Corporation Limited (DMRC), to start the operations at Yamuna Bank, Sukhdev Vihar, Jamia Millia Islamia, Jasola Vihar and Shaheen Bagh metro stations in Delhi. In Delhi Metro’s continued efforts to boost last-mile connectivity, the corporation will be further launching e-rickshaw facilities from 15 more metro stations by the end of next month.

15. GPS enabled vehicles.

Subject: Display / window advertisement dated 21.03.2021 relating to NIT / RFP regarding FAR work in Green Valley,
To: <indresh.sawhney@gmail.com>, <narendrabhalla403@gmail.com>


Dear Sh. Sawhney (President, MC) & Sh. Bhalla (Secy., MC),

With regard to the display / window advertisement dated 21.03.2021 relating to NIT / RFP regarding FAR work in Green Valley, I wish to make the following submissions :-

(i) In the meetings held in the recent past, it was decided in principle to follow the provisions of  GFR, 2017 in totality. However, the same has not been referred, which is very sad.  More disturbing point is that the tender has been floated in a hurry, without paying heed to my suggestions.

(ii) Less than 2 weeks' time has been given to the bidders / contractors for submission of the bids, whereas as per GFR minimum time to be given to the bidders for submission of bids is 3 weeks.

(iii) In the tender document, there is no mention of pre-bid meeting.

(iv) In spite of the fact that only 2 weeks' time has been given for submission of bids (which is not as per provisions of GFR), the NIT has not been uploaded on GV website.  In the circumstances, how can we expect getting good response from the bidders. 

The worst part is that the details regarding total FAR / Non FAR area, structural drawings, approved maps of the flats etc. don't find place in the NIT/RFP.  In the absence of the requisite details, how can be expect that good contracts would submit bids.   It seems that we don't need good numbers of bids.

(v) As per minutes of the AGM meeting dated 13.10.2019, the tentative cost relating to FAR work was Rs.18.30 Crores.  In the meeting called by you on 15.03.2021 in the Community Centre, it was apprised that in the wake of hike in prices of cement and steel, project cost may go up approximately by 10%.  Going by that, the estimated price could have been around Rs.20 Crores and not 25 Crores.  

I believe, despite all odds , members of the GV should have been taken into confidence before releasing the NIT with estimated cost of Rs. 25.11 Cr.., .

(vi)    In the meeting called by you on 15.03.2021, I had requested inter-alia for providing estimated cost of the FAR project of GV on the basis of per square foot area also (in addition to the estimated cost worked out on the basis of schedule of quantities).  The intention was to have an idea as to which option is more economical.

2.     In the end, I would like you to intimate composition of the Tender Commitee which shall evaluate the technical bids of the bidders / contractors on 04.04.2021.


(Naresh Kumar Sharma)
I-701, Green Valley CGHS Ltd.

QRyde Fleets - On Lease with VTS and drivers (these are services)
QRyde VTS (people who already have EVs)
Remember, we need to identify what the people want and then we will provide them the solution not that we build first and then sell!!!!!

Now, here is some Gyan. May or may not be available in University management books. Only experience teaches this. We now need to think :
Who can be our customers? - You scoped out JNU, GGSIP, DU. Try to think of places where a lot of movement of people and goods is there.
How will we approach these prospective customers? - Cold calling / telemarketing/ referrals/ tenders/ Email campaigns

Do you understand what a cold call means?
What is the relevance of telesales?
What is the art of opening a channel of discussion with a prospective client whom you have never interacted with. How do you convince someone in 2 minutes to give you his time?
What is the foremost principle of selling. Need to learn the difference between sales and marketing?
How does CRM differ from sales? 
Do you understand what re-acquisition of customers means?
Do you know that the most successful business entrepreneurs at times said that they never did any sales? They provided solutions. What does it mean?

25/05/21, 12:10 - Anuj Gupta: ***घर के ब्लैक फंगस से सावधान***

बाजार से आप प्याज खरीद कर लाते हैं कभी आपने देखा होगा उसके ऊपर काली-काली परत जमी रहती है।

असल में यही ब्लैक फंगस (काला फफूंद) होता है।

अआप अपने घरों के फ्रिज के दरवाजे खोलिए उसमें एक रबर लगी मिलेगी।

उस रबर को साफ रखें एवं फ्रिजर को साफ रखें अगर काला काला फंगस दिख रहा हो तो तत्काल उसकी अच्छे ढंग से सफाई कर दें और बराबर उसकी सफाई पर ध्यान दें।

उस रबर पर वो जो काला काला है वही है म्यूकोर्म्यूकोसिस यानी ब्लैक फंगस

अगर आपने ध्यान न दिया तो ये फंगस आपके फ्रिज के अंदर रखे खाद्य पदार्थों के माध्यम से बेहद आसानी से आपके अंदर प्रवेश कर सकता है।

★आटा गूंथ कर फ्रिज में ना रखें।
★ कटे फल फ्रिज में ना रखें।
★प्याज ताजा काटकर खाए, कटा प्याज देर तक ना रखें।
★फ्रिज में रखी हुई ब्रेड कत्तई यूज न करें।
★ए.सी. इस्तेमाल कम से कम करें।

सब कुछ ताजा और तुंरन्त इस्तेमाल करें।
और जिस भी खाद्य पदार्थ पर आपको काला काला फंगस जैसा कुछ भी दिखे उसको तुरन्त सावधानी से नष्ट कर दें।

अपने कूलर, एसी और आरओ मशीन की टोटी भी चेक करते रहिएगा।

बेहद चौकन्ना रहिए, चीजों के बारे में पढ़ते-लिखते रहिए और अपडेट रहिए, चित्त बिल्कुल शांत रखिए, शुद्ध खान पान से इम्युनिटी मजबूत रखिए, और व्यायाम करते रहें और हमेशा सकारात्मक रहें।

30/05/21, 21:05 - Anuj Gupta: Dear Residents ,

The Green Valley Family in the past few weeks has faced lot of anxious moments and has been burdened with lot of extra work on our shoulders due to the pandemic. 
We are grateful to the members and their families that after scores of Covid positive cases in the 4th week of April, we presently do not have any Covid positive cases in the society and this has only been made possible with the kind cooperation of one and all.
Keeping in mind the current situation and the Delhi Disaster Management Authority’s SOPs vide its letter no. No. F.2/07/2020/pt file-111/431 dt 29/5/2021 stating as per para 3 as under:- 
“And whereas, the situation of COVID-19 in NCT of Delhi has again been reviewed and observed that, though the number of COVID-19 patients and positivity rate is declining, the situation is still precarious.”
We too know of the above fact, as stated by DDMA above and In furtherance to our earlier advisories on Maids and other helps, the same restrictions shall continue. 
Keeping the long term measure, safety in mind and for convenience, we have scheduled a Covid Vaccination Camp in the Green Valley Society premises on Saturday, 5th June – for age category 18 and above, covishield vaccine priced at ₹1100 per jab.
We advise all those eligible to avail of this facility. 
Keeping the safety of all residents in mind, those who wish to avail of the following services :- Maids, cooks, drivers, vehicle cleaners need to mandatorily get their helps vaccinated at Govt . Centers or at Green Valley Vaccination Camp and submit a copy of the vaccination certificate of all family member and the help to the Green Valley office so as to grant approval of the same.
For residents who are not eligible for vaccination due to any medical reason, exemption from submitting their vaccination certificate will be approved on case to case basis. 
For those who are already availing services of help, they also need to submit their family as well as help’s vaccination certificates by 5th evening to continue availing these services. 
We understand that not all helps will be able to get themselves vaccinated due to various constraints, the Society has decided to subsidise 50% of the vaccination cost for maids and car cleaners at the vaccination drive in the society. Residents are urged to come forward and cover the remaining cost for their domestic helps.
We understand that while the cases have shown a downward trend, our precautions are still to be upheld with maximum strictness so that no further complications may arise. 
We look forward to your cooperation as always and especially in times of this unprecedented pandemic to help all in the community to be safe. We once again request all residents to adhere to covid protocol appropriate behaviour viz. wearing of masks, maintaining social distancing et al. 

With regards

03/06/21, 17:49 - Anuj Gupta: Dear Residents ,

The Green Valley Family in the past few weeks has faced lot of anxious moments and has been burdened with lot of extra work on our shoulders due to the pandemic. 
We are grateful to the members and their families that after scores of Covid positive cases in the 4th week of April, we presently do not have any Covid positive cases in the society and this has only been made possible with the kind cooperation of one and all.
Keeping in mind the current situation and the Delhi Disaster Management Authority’s SOPs vide its letter no. No. F.2/07/2020/pt file-111/431 dt 29/5/2021 stating as per para 3 as under:- 
“And whereas, the situation of COVID-19 in NCT of Delhi has again been reviewed and observed that, though the number of COVID-19 patients and positivity rate is declining, the situation is still precarious.”
We too know of the above fact, as stated by DDMA above and In furtherance to our earlier advisories on Maids and other helps, the same restrictions shall continue. 
Keeping the long term measure, safety in mind and for convenience, we have scheduled a Covid Vaccination Camp in the Green Valley Society premises on Saturday, 5th June – for age category 18 and above, covishield vaccine priced at ₹1100 per jab.
We advise all those eligible to avail of this facility. 
Keeping the safety of all residents in mind, those who wish to avail of the following services :- Maids, cooks, drivers, vehicle cleaners need to mandatorily get their helps vaccinated at Govt . Centers or at Green Valley Vaccination Camp and submit a copy of the vaccination certificate of all family member and the help to the Green Valley office so as to grant approval of the same.
For residents who are not eligible for vaccination due to any medical reason, exemption from submitting their vaccination certificate will be approved on case to case basis. 
For those who are already availing services of help, they also need to submit their family as well as help’s vaccination certificates by 5th evening to continue availing these services. 
We understand that not all helps will be able to get themselves vaccinated due to various constraints, the Society has decided to subsidise 50% of the vaccination cost for maids and car cleaners at the vaccination drive in the society. Residents are urged to come forward and cover the remaining cost for their domestic helps.
We understand that while the cases have shown a downward trend, our precautions are still to be upheld with maximum strictness so that no further complications may arise. 
We look forward to your cooperation as always and especially in times of this unprecedented pandemic to help all in the community to be safe. We once again request all residents to adhere to covid protocol appropriate behaviour viz. wearing of masks, maintaining social distancing et al. 

With regards

11/11/21, 00:07 - Anuj Gupta: For the first time in many years, I realised the meaning of true friendship. It was the tragic time period of the month of May when the Covid 2nd wave was on the peak. There was a lot of tension in my house. With God's grace, we were all doing fine but the situation was not the same with our relations. My mother fell ill with some stomach infection and father was over occupied with the business work and managing the household affairs. We really needed someone to help us out in this tough time. My grandmother who doesn't do much of the work at home also refused to cooperate. Now, the only option was to get a maid at home to do household work and prepare the meals for us. It was not safe due to the Covid scare and moreover, we were not in favor. 
I was crying one day and my friend Saanvi saw me. She came to me and asked about things. I could not hold my tears and explained the scenario of things. Saanvi told me that she would help me. She discussed the issue with her mother. She called up Mom and understood her situation. From that day and for the next one week, Saanvi's mother prepared the food for the entire entire family twice a day and sent it in tiffins to us. We tried telling them not to do it but still they did it. Not only this, they sent tea and coffee too for all. We were all overwhelmed with this gesture. 
It was a wonderful experience and for the first time, I realised the true meaning of friendship. Saanvi is so dear to me and we have been friends for the past 5 years. She always used to tell me that one day she would do something great for me. The days had come. She proved it. My mother recovered. She is doing fine now. I am so grateful to my true friend. She made this saying true - A friend in need is a friend indeed. 
Not only this, her mother came to my house too once and asked for the well being of all. At times, when people were keeping to themselves, they came up and helped us. God bless them. Full of gratitude for them.

21/11/21, 01:21 - Anuj Gupta: *The Covid 19 Pandemic and Mental Health - Article on Journal of Social work values and ethics*

Covid 19 has changed the lives of the people across the globe. It has had a huge impact on the entire ecosystem, thereby, impacting the economy, social and cultural life and also various other aspects of human mankind. While human life has changed all over, the state of physical and mental health of people has raised enormous concerns and is now a big center of focus with a lot of work around.

Now, let us give some thoughts to the subject of our ethics and responsibilities as being responsible citizens and social beings. There is a famous saying that the charity begins at home. The first lesson of life is taught at home. The first successful assignment where one delivers required results is carried out at home only. So, when we talk about social work values and ethics in this Covid era, we need to first understand what we are supposed to do first when the discussion is focussed on this mega topic.

To err is a human and a human is a social being. We live in an environment where we are surrounded by people, connected to each other through personal or social or business relationships. This ecosystem is called society and thus, each one of us is driven by social values and ethics. 

Our objective is to understand as to what are we required to follow or deliver in a scenario which is driven by the Pandemic impact.

Our first step towards delivering our responsibilities is to understand what are the DOs and DON'Ts. Are we taking care of these points? Can we keep others healthy if we ourselves are not healthy? Certainly, if we have a disease which can spread, we can contaminate the environment and others can get that too. So, here is the basic ethic to be followed first of all. Wear masks while you are in public. Your safety is primary and that will keep others safe too. If somebody does not wear a mask, ask the person to do so and do not support someone who is not doing so. Do not ever indulge into public interaction without following this protocol.

Next, is to ensure that you get vaccinated. Also, motivate /educate others too to do so. There is a famous saying - Each one teaches one. So follow this and cultivate this chain of vaccinated people. 

Prevention is always better than cure. What is it that we can do to have a healthy environment. The answer is to have healthy people around. Let us increase the awareness to follow methods to stay healthy. Let us make physical exercise and Yoga a regular part of life. These will increase the immunity and less chances of contracting the infection. As a responsible and caring society member, we should focus on these and guide at least our own family members to follow these.

Think of people who have suffered from this disease. Many of them recovered. Many lost lives. Many lost their near and dear ones. Think of the mental agony which these people have passed through. Our values tell us that we should support them to whatever extent we can. Give them mental support at least. If possible, provide financial assistance too to the needy ones if feasible. If you are a business service provider, provide goods/services at economical prices to the people who cannot pay much. If you are an employer, ensure that you do not lay off people as currently the economy is affected and there are not many jobs in the market. So, do not snatch somebody's bread. If you are a medical practitioner, ensure that you do not work to charge more money from the patients. Try to provide best treatments and if possible, give concessions to people who cannot pay much. Same for the hospital owners and diagnostic centers.

A lot of people have been working from home during this pandemic. There have been situations where families are happy to have their dear ones in front of their eyes at home and working. People have developed better understanding. But there have been other things too. The friction has increased in the family members and relationships are affected thereby resulting in deterioration of their emotional bonding. The pandemic has seen splits in the families just because of the people not valuing the safe being of their dear ones as they have been working from home and are in front of their eyes. Our values state that we need to value people and respect their dignity and give them due respect which they deserve. Everyone plays a vital role in the family and no one is more or less important.

It is very important to be a responsible citizen of the country. Our ethics tell us that we should follow the protocols. We should pay taxes on time. Covid has put an immense burden on the Government and they have been doing a lot of work. We should support wherever we can to the best. 

We should promote a green environment. Try to control pollution. Use electric vehicles as much as possible. While the majority of the population uses petrol and diesel vehicles, we should ensure that our vehicles do not emit pollution. Get these serviced regularly. Ensure that you have a valid pollution control certificate for the vehicles.

So, overall, our focus should be to build an environment around us where we can stay healthy, keep others healthy, be happy and keep others happy, eat well, sleep well and let others do so. So, the time is now to consider the whole planet as a family, our society. AND, another important thing, cultivate greenery. Plant trees. If not trees, at least have plants at home. Breathe fresh air. Eat vegetarian food, healthy food. Stop drinking alcohol and educate others too. Have positive thoughts and spread positive vibes in people. Have faith in God and spread positivity around.

Remember, life comes only once. Live it to the fullest, to the best and to the best of your cultural and social values with high morale and ethics. Good Day!

19/12/21, 11:42 - Anuj Gupta: King Harshavardhan was defeated in the battle.

He was handcuffed and taken to the winner king.At that time the winner king was in a happy mood.

The king kept a proposal for Harshavardhan and said, “ If you can answer me a question correctly I will return your kingdom or else leave aside the kingdom, you shall have to remain a prisoner for the rest of your life in my country.”

“ The question is, ' what does a woman want from her man?' You will get a month of time to give the answer.”

Harshavardhan accepted the King's proposal.

He went to various places and met many scholars, preachers, priests, dancers,prostitutes, housewives,maids and many more to know what exactly a woman wants from a man.

If someone said she wants ornaments, the other would say she wants children from her man, another said beautiful house and family, yet another said she would like to have the throne etc. etc.

Harshavardhan was not satisfied with these answers at all.

The month was about to end.

On the other hand, Harshavardhan was unable to collect a satisfactory answer.

Then someone informed that far away,in another country there lives a witch. Only she can give proper answer to this question because she has all the answers.

Along with friend Siddhiraj, Harshavardhan went and met the witch. He asked the question.

The witch said , “ I will give you the correct answer only if your friend agrees to marry me.”

The witch was old and extremely ugly. He didn't want this injustice to happen with his friend.

But to save his friend and the king of his country, Siddhiraj gave his consent to marry the witch and the marriage happened.

The witch then answered Harshavardhan and said, “ A woman wants to be independent so that she can take decisions on her own.”

Harshavardhan liked the answer.

He told this answer to the winner king. The king liked the answer, released Harshavardhan and returned his kingdom to him.

On the other hand, the witch on her wedding night said to her husband, “You have a pure heart. You have sacrificed yourself to save your friend, so, I want to tell you something.”

“Everyday, I look ugly for 12 hours and extremely beautiful for the next 12 hours. Tell me, which look would you like to accept.”

Siddhiraj said, “ That is your decision dear. I have accepted you as my wife,so, I would like you anyway. ”

Hearing this, the witch transformed into a beauty and said, “ You have allowed me to take the decision, therefore, from now I shall always remain beautiful.”

“Actually this is my real look. I had changed my appearance into ugly witch for the ugly people all around.”

*******************************************

The social norms have made women dependent,but, mentally no woman accepts dependence.

Hence,those homes who have given power to the wives are generally happier.

We may not allow the wife to be the head of the house,but, we should atleast release half part of her life, that half part, in which she can openly take her own decisions

27/01/22, 17:37 - Mommy: F𝐢𝐧𝐚lly something practical and honest!  Minister of Health of Portugal, Marta Temido delivers the reality:

1. We may have to live with COVID 19 for months or years. Let's *not* deny it or panic. Let's *not* make our lives useless. *Let's learn to live with that fact*.

2. *You can't destroy* the COVID19 viruses that have penetrated cell walls by drinking gallons of hot water -  *you're just going* to the bathroom more often.

3. *Washing your hands is the best method* for your protection.

4. If you *do not have* a COVID19 patient at home, there is *no need* to disinfect your home surfaces.

5. Packed cargoes, gas pumps, shopping carts and ATMs do not cause infection.  *Wash your hands*, live your life as usual.

6. COVID19 *is not a foodborne* infection. It is associated with *infection drops* like the flu. There is *no* demonstrated risk that COVID19 is *transmitted* through food.

7. You *can* lose your sense of smell with many allergies and viral infections. This is *just* a non-specific *symptom* of COVID19.

8. Once home, you *don't need* to urgently change your clothes and shower! Purity is a virtue, *paranoia is not!*

9. The COVID19 virus *is not* in the air. This is a respiratory droplet infection that requires *close contact*.

10. The air is clean, you *can walk* through the gardens, through the parks, just *avoid crowding*.

11. It is sufficient to use *normal soap* against COVID19, not antibacterial soap. This is a *virus, not a bacteria*.

12. You *don't have to* worry about your food orders. But you can heat everything in the microwave if you wish.

13. The *chances* of *taking the
COVID19 *home with the *shoes* is *like being struck* by lightning twice a day. I've been working against viruses for 20 years -  *infections* by droplets do *not* spread like that!

14. You *cannot* be protected from the virus by drinking vinegar, sugarcane juice and ginger! These *are for immunity*, not healing.

15. Wearing a mask for long periods *interferes* with *breathing and oxygen levels*.   *Only* use it in a crowd.

16. Wearing *gloves* is also a *bad idea*; the virus can accumulate on the glove and be easily transmitted if you *touch your face*.  Better to *just* wash your hands regularly.

17. *Immunity* is greatly weakened by *always remaining* in a sterile environment. Even if you eat immunity-boosting foods, *regularly leave your house* for any park/beach. *Immunity is increased* by exposure to pathogens, not by staying home and consuming fried/spicy/sweetened foods and carbonated beverages, and not engaging in physical activity.

Source:
 https://www.impala.pt/noticias/atualidade/covid-19

05/05/22, 22:16 - Anuj Gupta: The summer of 2021, a very different season that year. This year was completely different and brought a lot of painful memories in life. We saw things, came across experiences which we had not felt ever in our entire life time. It was the beginning of April and that was the time when I had a feeling of slight respite that life had begun to stabilize after going through that nightmare of Covid era which had hit the world last year in March 2020. 

People had almost given up using masks and life seemed to be going on at a normal pace and everyone had a thought that Covid was gone and we could actually forget it like another pandemic which was successfully addressed.

Destiny had something else in store for everyone!!!!!!!!!!!

The month of April began and the weather as usual had started becoming hot, temperature rising and everyone thought that this summer will again be like the one which was there 2 years back. Things started changing abruptly and we started seeing a spike in the number of Covid cases. Cases started increasing suddenly and the numbers began to multiply everyday. The 2nd wave of Covid was in. All of a sudden, life changed again. Lockdown was declared and the educational institutes were closed. Companies once again implemented Work from Home but everything seemed to get into the place a bit late. The 2nd wave had crippled the lives of people and a large number of people had contracted the delta virus which was the new strain, a really deadly strain. 

There was hue and cry everywhere , scarcity of oxygen cylinders, shortage of beds in the hospitals, shortage of medicines for treating people and the situation became worse and the Pandemic got fierce. Being in a business family, we were completely dependent on the traditional way of running the business which was characterized   by direct sales and one to one interaction with the clients. There were huge losses but somehow we managed to cover up our expenses and got going with things.

Unfortunately, somebody in the house was contacted with the virus and our Uncle who was staying with us in our house at that time got severely ill. He was found to be delta positive. We had a huge panic at home and everyone was grief stricken. We somehow worked to maintain social distance and started the treatment for Uncle. Everyone else got quarantined and we somehow got alright after 3 days of fever. We took plenty of hot water and vitamins , did yoga and became alright. 

Medical situation became severe and his oxygen level went down. It was a critical situation and there were no beds available anywhere. We didn't know what to do and where to go. Nothing was working for him. This was a time when we actually realised the hardship of life. We used to get phone calls everyday from relatives and friends and they asked for well being but nobody had any solution. We realised that nobody could do anything and it was all up to the Almighty. Then an Angel appeared on the scene. We had a neighbour who stayed 5 houses away from us. To the best of our surprise, he is a person with whom we hardly had any interaction and he was new in the area. One day, my mother was going to the temple and he suddenly asked who everyone was at home and he had not seen anyone in the vicinity since a week. Mother started weeping and narrated the whole hardship the family faced. And now, it was a new chapter of life which began.

That Uncle visited our place and assured his best help. He brought lunch and dinner for everyone in the house and carried on for the next one week. He was working in a Pharma company and he arranged a nurse and doctor who visited our house and provided oxygen arrangement to Uncle who was ill. The doctor started treating Uncle and his oxygen level started stabilising. The medicines started working and it was a real miracle that took place. His family took care of so well and arranged food, medicines , treatment and every essentials and things improved. Uncle was out of danger and health was okay. He had recovered. Everyone at home had a sigh of relief and everyone was also doing fine.

This person had come like an angel and soon we realised that the faith we had in Almighty was really a Universal Truth. God helped us in his form as he became his angel. I wonder at times as to what was his interest in doing all this. Instead he put his life at risk but he had only one agenda - to be a human and extend the best of this help. He lived to his values and did what he thought was right. Do good and help others. No objective of earning any money and only thought was to be a good human. Do we really have such angels in today's materialistic world? It is amazing. All We feel and pray to God is to bless him with all the health, wealth and happiness in his life. The time of this month of April and May was terrible and many members in the family might have struggled to survive but destiny had something else in store for us. Our good deeds paid, our faith in God paid and we came out of that nightmare. 

Life was restored back to normal. Time changed. Business improved. Health improved. But still today when I think about those days, I am not able to believe how we can have such angels among us in today's materialistic world. 

We all at times boast of our relations, our money, our contacts , our influence. Where does all that go when you actually need help in tough situations? There is a famous saying that as and when a ship starts drowning, at first the rats run away from the ship. So, when we are in trouble, is it a fact that the so-called best of the relatives shut their doors first. Are they friends in need or are they friends in good times and just neighbors in bad times who don't open their doors.

This is how this world is. People call up just to let the other person know as to what great they have done in their lives. Who bothers to actually ask someone if they need help any time. Rather they tend to step away when there is a need. So, very few people in this world understand the meaning of real humanity and they come to rescue when someone actually needs it. 

That Uncle did this for us. We shall always be grateful to him for what all he did to us. May God bless him with all prosperity in life.

03/06/22, 14:09 - Mommy: *Dr. Milind Kulkarni HR L&T*
Just because I am holding a senior position in HR with L&T, I have been getting many requests from my relatives, friends,  acquaintances, to help their sons or daughters, who have freshly passed out from engineering college, to get job in L&T. The number of requests are huge. So many fresh engineers are unemployed, I could hardly helped only few of them to get job in L&T or in some other companies where I have contacts. I feel bad to say NO to many of the requests or for those whom I can't help. They get disappointed... I can understand. Parents invest their life time earned money just to see their sons or daughters getting degree in engineering.

They think that jobs are easily available for engineers. After interviewing many of them, I can't even tell them  that your son or daughter do not even have minimum required technical knowledge. Getting first class or distinction has become so easy without having fundamental knowledge of engineering. *It's high time for parents to stop running behind engineering degrees.*

*USA produces around 1 lakh engineers per year for a $16 trillion economy.*
*India produces 15 lakhs engineers for a $2 trillion economy.* 
The earlier mass recruiting sector was Manufacturing. It used to recruit from the core branches like Electrical, Mechanical, Civil etc. But, Manufacturing is relatively stagnant at 17% of the GDP. So the core branch placements have become very difficult. 
The more recent mass recruiter was the IT sector. It grew from scratch to almost 5% of the GDP in a short time. IT Employed millions of engineers. 

Now, IT is also saturating. Only good, skilled IT Engineers are in demand. 
If you look at the sectoral composition of Indian economy, most of the sectors do not need engineers. Tourism is 10% of the GDP, does not require engineers. Financial sector, Trade, Hotels and Restaurants do not require engineers. Requirement of engineers in Health, Education, Agriculture is also negligible. 

*More than 50% of the GDP has no role for Engineers.* Still most of Indian youth are becoming Engineers. The situation is not sustainable . 
Demand is low while supply is high. Over and above this, skill level of an average engineer is poor, almost its non-existent in many cases. If we leave aside the top 100–200 colleges, most fresh engineers have no idea of what they studied. Ask a fresh mechanical engineer, can s/he design a simple frame? 

Today the situation is that most engineers are working in a field that has no connection to what they have studied in the college. This is a waste of resources. 
Engineering degree does not come cheap. It costs about 10-15 lakhs. For poor parents, its a huge burden. When their son / daughter is not able to secure a job, they are devastated. 

For the nation, you can calculate the loss. Leave around 1 lakh engineers that NASSCOM says are employable. The rest 14 lakhs have each wasted 10 lakhs of fees. That totals to around $20 Billion. Almost equal to the Government’s spending on healthcare. Over this, there is loss of human capital. 
India needs to replan the whole engineering education system. Goverment need to  cut down on the number of colleges and improve the quality in the rest. 

*Also students should explore other career options than everyone becoming Engineers.* 

When it comes to education, a multitude of options are available today! From Aviation, to Hotel Management, Short Term Programs to big movie production courses, Data science, cyber security, Information Security, Cloud Technology Designing, Indian Armed Forces, Animation and VFX, Digital Marketing, Film Making, Technology Courses like SQL, PHP, Big Data, C, C++, etc. and much more! 
For a majority of courses like these, there are entrance exams too, such as the NATA, CEED, NID entrance, NIFT entrance, NDA entrance, MBA Entrance, Hotel Management entrance, CET, NEET and many more! Here, the right training goes a long way in getting your child admission to their dream institute! *Do you know what are the top career tracks of 2022 other than engineering??* See the following list.
1. Animation, VFX and Multimedia
2. Fashion Design, Event Management and Interior decoration.
3. Aeronautical and Aviation
4.  Film making, Script Writing and Acting.
5. IT, cloud and data science.
6. Networking, information security.
7. Beauty, Modelling and Cosmetology
8. Fitness, dietitian and nutritionist
9. Foreign languages.
10. Music and Dance.

*Please share this with your relatives /friends / 12th pass students and help them in planning their education and carrer appropriately than madly running after engineering admissions!!

15/06/22, 18:25 - Anuj Gupta: If I could change three things in the country, what would those be? This is a million dollar question and I would love to answer it. 

However, before I consider answering this great question, let us do some retrospection of the events and developments/ trends of the past few decades.
 
India is a land of diversity. We have a population of nearly 1.7 billion and have people living in villages and towns, with different mindsets, different cultures, educational backgrounds, 
different religions, different philosophies etc. So, the lives of people are characterized with different challenges and different approaches.

Well, when talking of changing something in such a big demographic, we need to consider the impact of bringing the change. Are people susceptible to change? Is change going to be smooth ?
Every change may have some goal but the results may not be aligned to the desired outcomes.

I think, with all said above, the focus areas change could be Education system, Medical Ecosystem, Infrastructure, Economy, Technology Trends.  

I would like to focus on the Education system, Medical Ecosystem and another subject which explains how to live our lives with leisure and satisfaction. In other words, how to take the best out of 
whatever we do.

Now, the first subject : Education System!

This is a very generic topic and I guess, almost everyone will have diversified thoughts on this. I would like to emphasize that when I say this topic, I am not talking of the way admissions are made in colleges or the courses are structured or how the fee is decided for the courses. My concern is as to how we develop quality and skilled professionals who can be efficient and responsible citizens of the country 
and can help the human mankind in solving the complex problems which could be from the daily life, business world, medical science or engineering etc.

So, let us analyze a bit. When a student enrolls in a school or college, what is their goal? They are taught only one thing in school - get good marks and try to achieve number one position. also, they are 
motivated to focus on their health too. When one joins a college - their goal is to get a good job or enrol in a good degree in higher studies and make money.

Can we think something beyond this. Is earning money the only goal of life? 

Have we ever thought about what we should be doing? We live in a family. We are answerable to our family and have responsibilities. Then we have responsibilities towards our society, our country and then the entire humanity.

Should we not be explained right from day one as when we join our school or college that we should identify one goal of our life? We should be made to analyze what it is that we can do the best?
Which are the complex problems around us that we can solve and accordingly work? Should we not be made to understand that we need not run after money. If we have value in our work, money will
itself come to us.

Instead what we are explained to do - WE ALL SERVE OR MADE TO DREAM TO SERVE A VERY SMALL SEGMENT OF THE SOCIETY WHO JUST USE OUR SKILLS AND MAKE MONEY AND IN
RETURN PAY US SOME PART OF IT!!!!!

I would like to add to the education system a lot more practical study of the environment. Everybody should be educated in a way that one understands how to solve problems and not create problems
for someone to solve. We need to learn how to do things ourselves , instead of depending on others for everything.

Does current education teach us or train us as to how we can follow protocols in our daily life?

Tell me why we do not use a helmet while driving a two wheeler or when we are sitting with someone on it? Why can't we use masks in Covid Era? Why do we tend to overspeed and reach early?
How many of us remember this - BETTER LATE THAN NEVER! There would be numerous examples from all walks of life.

Have we ever focussed on the fact that our body needs healthy food and what do we eat??? Do we ever think of keeping our health in good condition?

So, I would like to bring about this change in Education system. LET EDUCATION TEACH US HOW TO LIVE A SIMPLE, DISCIPLINED AND HEALTHY LIFE AND MAKE US MATURE TO REALIZE 
WHAT COULD BE THE BEST SUBJECT FOR US WHERE WE CAN BUILD A CAREER AND THAT WOULD HELP US AND EVERY ONE!

The 2nd subject that I would want to focus upon is MEDICAL ECOSYSTEM.

In India, the foremost thing a person does when one falls ill is to connect with a doctor. We are very quick to find the most suitable doctor which can treat our ailment. My question is that as and when 
somebody is ill and gets treated and returns back to the normal life; HAVE THEY EVER DONE A RETROSPECTION AS TO WHAT COULD BE DONE TO ERADICATE THIS HEALTH ISSUE SO THAT
IT DOES NOT RECUR?

We are very intelligent to remember the medicines, identify the best specialists but how many of us work to improve our health?

Now the other side of it. Doctors write prescriptions , give the best medicines. How many of them educate the patients that some small steps can help them to avoid health issues?

Should we not have a centralized system where everyone is registered through a unique ID and a health record is maintained. Time to time, they should be sent reminders through SMS or email that they should get their tests done and consult doctors. They should have their health scores available to them. This all can be managed using Data Science and AI.

Last, but not the least, I would like to explain to everyone that we need to understand the meaning of Life. Do not run after money. Have values in your life. Do good and be good to others. Follow discipline 
and live everyday with positivity.

I would like to increase social awareness among people. Think of your neighbors and friends as your families. Take care of your responsibilities. Respect relations, respect everyone! Do good for the people around and overall, become a good human!

26/06/22, 12:58 - Mommy: FastTag Scam Alert - झूठ या सच??

आज एक वीडियो देखा, उसमे 2 नवयुवक car में बैठे हैं, तभी एक लड़का उनकी car का windscreen साफ करने आता है... वो bonut पर चढ़ जाता है, फिर हाथ में पहनी हुई घड़ी दिखाता है.. इतने में एक लड़का शोर मचाने लगता है... पकड़ो पकड़ो.

वो बच्चे को नहीं पकड़ पाते... बाद में ड्राइव कर रहा युवक बताता है कि ये नया scam है, जिसमें एक gang छोटे बच्चो को High Tech घड़िया दे देता है.. फिर वो बच्चे आपकी car कि सफाई करने का बहाना मार कर आपके fasttag को अपनी घड़ी से scan कर लेते हैं.. और आपका wallet खाली हो जाता है.

Social media की मेहरबानी से ये वीडियो पूरी दुनिया में वायरल हो रहा है... लोग बिना जानकारी इसे फैला रहे हैं.. और बेवजह डर रहे हैं.

इसका एक ही शब्द में अगर सच जानना है... तो वो यह है की ये वीडियो 'Fake' बनाया हुआ है... ऐसा कोई FastTag scam नहीं होता.

अब आप पूछेंगे कि ऐसा कैसे???

पहले आप Technology को समझिये.

आपकी गाड़ी में एक FastTag लगा होता है... उसमे एक छोटी सी  RFID Chip होती है, एक antenna होता है.... बहुत छोटा होता है... Tag की दोनों layers के बीच में होता है. इस chip में आपकी गाड़ी की जानकारी होती है... और Backend से आपका NHAI wallet, Paytm Wallet या आपकी Bank के account की जानकारी इसमें Coded होती है.

दूसरे छोर पर होता है NHAI.... जो आपसे Toll वसूलता है... हर टोलप्लाजा पर एक scanner होता है.. जो आपके गाड़ी के FastTag को स्कैन करके Payment वसूलता है. जाहिर है Payment NHAI के bank account में ही जायेगा...... इसका अर्थ है Background में NHAI का बैंक account Connect होता है... जो भी पैसा कटेगा वो सीधा NHAI के account में ही जायेगा... अड़ोस पड़ोस वाले किसी अंकल के account में नहीं जा सकता... क्यूंकि इसकी programming ही ऐसे हुई है.

FastTag से पैसा कैसे Deduct होता है??
आपकी car में जो FastTag RFID chip होती है.. वो एक Passive Chip होती है... मतलब उसमे कोई Power source या Battery नहीं connect होती.....जैसे ही आप अपनी car को Toll Plaza पर लगे हुए Scanner के एक ख़ास Radius में लाते हैं... वो scanner आपके RFID पर signal डालता है... और आपका RFID सारी जानकारी Scanner को Transmit कर देता है..... और जितने पैसे कटने होते हैं.. वो Signal आपकी बैंक account या wallet को चला जाता है.

आपके Wallet या Account से NHAI को payment कैसे जाता है??

Backend में NCPI का जबरदस्त  इंफ्रास्ट्रक्चर काम करता है.... वही आपके account की जानकारी रखता है... और जैसे ही टोलप्लाजा का Scanner Fasttag को read करता है... अगर Tag सही है, Blacklist नहीं है.. उसमे Balance है.. तो वो NCPI को instruction दे देता है... कि ग्राहक के account से इतनी रकम काटो....

Background में NCPI का UPI या बैंकिंग payment system उतनी रकम आपके Wallet या Account से NHAI के account में transfer कर देता है.

और थोड़ी देर में आपको msg भी आता है... कि NHAI के इस Highway के Toll से आपके इतने रूपए कटे, और इतना balance बचा है.

अब आप सोचिये.... जब आपका RFID coded है, उसे टोलप्लाजा पर लगे scanner के अलावा कोई डिवाइस पढ़ नहीं सकती....... उधर Scanner पर NHAI का account नंबर ही Fixed हो रखा है..... मतलब जो भी पैसा जायेगा वो NHAI के account में ही जायेगा..

ऐसे में कोई बच्चा, पालिका बाजार मे 50 रूपए की 2 दर्जन मिलने वाली फर्जी घड़ी पहन कर.. आपकी गाड़ी के bonut पर Locking Popping करके scan करके आपके account से पैसा उड़ा लेगा?? मतलब आपके हिसाब से यह संभव है 😂😂😂

और अगर यह इतना ही आसान है... तो कोई भी parking में खड़ी गाड़ियों से ना कर लेगा scan???  सुबह से शाम तक पालिका बाजार या खान मार्केट की parking में scan करो.. शाम तक करोड़पति बन जाओ.... बढ़िया स्कीम है भाई लोग 😂😂

इसलिए कहा गया है... दिखावो पर मत जाओ.. अपनी अक्ल लगाओ..... वैसे वो वीडियो बनाने वाले पर सुना है FIR हो गयी है.... पुलिस जल्दी ही उसका FastTag सुजायेगी 😀

घर जाने के लिए निकला। अशांत और विचलित मन लिए सब्जी मंडी पहुँचा कुछ सब्जियाँ खरीदीं।

आज कुछ देर हो गई थी तो घर पहुँचकर खिचड़ी अथवा मैगी बना लेने का विचार चल रहा था। पिछले सप्ताह के एक भी कपड़े धुले नहीं थे अतः 5-6 दिन से एक ही जीन्स को रगड़ रहा था।

एक हाथ से काँधे पर लटके बैग को सम्हालता और दूसरे हाथ में दूध की थैली पकड़े पसीने से तरबतर चेहरा लिए घर पहुँचा। द्वार का ताला खोलना चाहा तो देखा, पल्ले भर भिड़के हुए थे, ताला खुला था। कुछ चिंतित हुआ।

जैसे ही घर में प्रवेश किया तो यूँ लगा मानो स्वर्ग में आ गया हूँ। शंका हुई कि, किसी दूसरे के घर में तो नहीं आ गया ? खामोशी से अंदर के कमरे में गया। फ्रीज खोला तो भीतर की ठंडक चेहरे से टकराई। कोने में अचार रखा हुआ था। मैथी की भाजी बारीक और व्यवस्थित कतरी हुई करीने से रखी थी। सुबह तो फ्रीज में एक ठो बिस्किट पैकेट रखने की जगह नहीं थी, सारा फ्रीज भरा पड़ा था और अब देखो, साफ सुथरी जगह ही जगह थी। धीरे से साथ लाई हुई सब्जियाँ भी फ्रीज में ही रख दीं।

कोने में रखी पानी की टंकी, जिसने हफ्ते भर से पानी का मुँह नहीं देखा था अब, पूरी भरी हुई चमक रही थी। तभी ध्यान गया कि पीछे पीछे अगरबत्ती की खुशबू भी चली आ रही थी, मन को आनंदित कर रही थी।

अपना बैग एक कुर्सी पर पटका तो याद आया कि, सुबह अपना टॉवेल बिस्तर पर ही छोड़ दिया था, देखा तो वहाँ न होकर वह खिड़की के बाहर तार पर लटका सूख रहा था। अलमारी का पल्ला खोला जिसमें बिना धुले कपड़े थे लेकिन अब सारे ही धुले, इस्त्री किए व्यवस्थित रखे थे।

सुबह एक रुमाल मिलकर नहीं दे रहा था और अब, अंदर साफसुथरे रुमाल पर रुमाल की गड्डी रखी हुई थी। सुबह सॉक्स की जोड़ी नहीं मिली तो अलग अलग डिजाइन के मोजे पहनकर निकल गया था लेकिन अब सारे सॉक्स एक स्थान पर उपस्थित पड़े मुझे देख मुस्कुरा रहे थे। लाल, पीली, नीली शर्ट्स बढ़िया हैंगर पर टंगी हुई थीं।

धीरे से टीवी के सामने बैठा, टीवी जिसपर धूल की परतें जम गई थीं अब चमक रहा था और स्क्रीन पर चित्र भी स्पष्ट दिख रहे थे। प्यास लगी तो पानी पीने किचिन में पहुँचा, जिस किचिन में लहसुन, प्याज और न जाने किस किस किस्म की गंध भरी रहती थी, अब  भूख जगा देने वाले भोजन की सुगंध से महक रहा था।

भावनाओं में बहता, बाहर आकर टीवी के सामने एक चेयर पर बैठ गया और अपनी आँखें बंद कर लीं और सोचने लगा। फिर आँखें खोलकर अपनी ही बाँह पर चिमटी ली कि, कहीं ये सब स्वप्न तो नहीं। तभी गरमागरम पकौड़ों की प्लेट और भाप निकलती चाय किसी ने सामने टेबल पर रख दी। भीतर का अहम जैसे जर्रा जर्रा होकर बिखर गया। जब थककर आता था तो जैसे तैसे दही चावल पर गुजारा कर लिया करता था और आज भाप निकलती स्वादिष्ट चाय और गरम पकौड़ों का आनंद ले रहा था। न चाहते हुए भी आँसू की दो बूंदें आँखों से निकलकर गालों पर बह निकलीं। फिर खुद को सम्हाला तो अहसास हुआ.....

Airbags are of no use if seat belt is not strapped which is the first line of defence. 

Air bag is the second line of defence only if the first is complied

If you do not lock sitting chair seat belt properly Air bag will not open

All the cars have rear seat belts as per government regulation, but very few people use them, it is an illusion that the rear is very safe. 

During the time of crash the person behind is sometimes thrown at a force of 40G (40 times the gravity, which means the person weighing 80kgs will be like 3200kgs). 

If the front passenger is wearing seat belt and rear passenger is not, during the time of crash the front passenger is likely to be severely injured or killed due to the rear passenger falling with a weight of an elephant. 

Totally surprised to hear this. Guys - We pay for seat belts - why not use them and be safe. 

Pl follow safety rules when you are travelling.

29/09/22, 11:41 - Anuj Gupta: 1. An interesting story and a real one, I was just taken back in the past. Do give a glance. Please bear with me for 2 minutes reading this.

2. The summer of 1984 and this was a wet afternoon with showers cooling down the temperature.

3. The 2nd half of the school was called off as the teachers got busy in some assignments.

4. Our PT teacher Mohan Duttji took us to the play ground and organised a race among all students.

5. We all stood in a row and as soon as he gave the signal , we started running. 

6. We had to touch the other end of the ground and come back to the start point.

7. I was a bit weak and soon got tired. 

8. Then I started looking at as to who was running beside me. I started competing with him to move ahead. But he raced ahead.

9. Then I started staring at all in the race and started thinking that there were so many ahead of me. 

10. I thought of running ahead of each of them and it started bothering me as to why so many were ahead of me.

11. Now my race was focused on moving ahead of each of them and I was looking at everyone.

12. Surprisingly, each one of them moved ahead of me and I was amongst the last ones who returned when the race closed. 

13. Out of 20 , I ranked 18 or 19. Only ones who were lethargic or fat were behind me.

14. I had lost the race.

15. I came home, cried and told the story to all.

16. He smiled at me and said……

17. “You had lost the race in the starting itself. You were only and only looking at others, comparing etc.”

18. “You lost your focus, your energy and got into stupidity of looking at others and comparison. This is where you lost the time.”

19. Moral of the Story: Focus on your path, ensure it is right, preserve energy, donot compare, donot get carried away by others’ achievements. 

20. Enhance your strength, reduce distractions and have a goal. Then, only you will win the race else you will lose it.”

24/10/22, 11:12 - Anuj Gupta: Human Relationships is a big subject and when it comes to analyzing this, it gets cumbersome to put thoughts together and arrive at a concrete analysis about what is what and how things change.

We all grow up, changes happen in life. People come and go, life goes on. One thing that draws a lot of attention at different times is how to cultivate and manage relationships?

Two brothers do not have a similar thought process. Couples have different perceptions. Parents and children have a generation gap. Friends do not arrive at a consensus. Business relationships, again different deliverables and expectations, hardly these are matched. Social life, again mismatch. Everywhere, you find something or the other does not align.

So, here are my questions. 

- Why can't relationships be freed of expectations and one big issue which is Egoism? 

- Is it so difficult to respect other people's thoughts and values?

- Why do we tend to become so judgemental and not leave things as they are?

- Why do we not simplify our relations and be original? Why so much show business?

- How many times do we tend to do self retrospection?

I think everyone needs to understand that humans are social beings and everyone is bonded to someone or more people in life.

We need relations to be with us in good and bad times. Giving up a relationship is easy , however difficult to build one. At the other end, what is the point if there is no respect in the bond?

Can everyone as a human simplify one's life and make life prosper by letting people know or understand that they care for them and respect them. Dynamics of the entire world will change!

Welcome the thoughts from all!

31/10/22, 13:46 - Anuj Gupta: Thought for today !

Change is an integral aspect of life Whether it is a change of place, change of status, change of locality, change of relations or anything else, the only thing which is constant in this world is change.

Gain and loss is a part of life, that is how the things work in life. Anything and everything that belongs to someone, may or may not stay forever along! Then what is it that lasts forever? A lot of retrospection required!!!

Human relationships are an ever happening subject and these never fade away with anything. Time changes, world changes, these keep going their way,

One beautiful relation is Friendship. We get friends in life, we get new dimensions, new experiences, new learnings and above all, we are empowered with the Godly power that blesses us every day, every moment and fills us with positivity.

I have diversified thoughts in this arena!

What is the meaning of friendship? Do we get REAL friends in today's world? What do we expect from friends? What if our expectations are not met? How do money matters get aligned with friendship?

Friend in need is a friend indeed. If someone is unable to help, does it go away? Difficult to define? 

My definition is that Friendship is a relationship all above the dynamics of the entire World's economy and ecosystems. Someone who teaches you how to live life to the best, shows you the path to become successful and gain prosperity in life, someone who does not cry with you but teaches you how to come out of pain and shed off the tears, someone who may not laugh with you but teaches you as to how to cherish each and every moment of life, keep your smile intact at every moment, someone who may not give you money but shows you the way to earn it with honesty, someone who might not hold your hold in crisis, but walks along and ensures that you do not fall, someone who transforms you into a contented person and helps you to take the best out of life is a FRIEND.

Nobody walks alone and everybody never stays along! Friends empower us!

So, we should understand this and analyse. Thoughts welcome from all!

01/11/22, 09:57 - Anuj Gupta: Here is a very important and integral aspect of our lives and it is more of one’s personality traits viz. Contentment. Let us talk about it and put thoughts together!

Have we ever thought as to how we could stay contented? We go through the journey of life, come across different stages, different people and pass through different situations. We all at some or the other point of time talk about what we have, what we lack and what we need further. Do we ever have this answer that one has got enough?

I think this is an ever progressing and unending debate. If we get contented, we shall stop thinking of growth. If we never get contented, we shall ever crib. However the question is then as to how to be happy because both ways we lose our cool and always get into circles of looking for one thing or other.

Let us take a tangent here. Let us answer one question to ourselves and not the rest of the world. Who is managing the entire world? Do we control anything in this world? We often tend to think that we control too many things but is it actually so?

I think we are all connected to each other one way or the other and some supernatural power governs us. What we think that we control is actually not in our hands. It is a part of sequences which get created as a result of our actions and decide the destiny. Input proportionates the output.

So, my thought would be that we should live the life to the best, every day is a new day and every moment brings a fresh lease of life. We need to cherish the time. Time never stops. So go with time. Be thankful to the Trinity for giving every moment to us and take the best out of it.

Recently I learnt a new thing. Get into get togethers with people who understand you and you get to know what they look for. Go for an outing, smile, laugh, eat, dance and spend quality time. Learn from them about their good things and improve in self. Socialism if managed well can get us great avenues and opportunities to progress better in life.

Contentment is nothing but a state of your mind. It is connected to your heart and soul. It does not come by spending money or building status or making the world admire you. It comes from within your soul , it is a message that your inner self gives you and fills you with happiness and positivity.

Start loving and valuing yourself, get into things which you are passionate about, eat the food of your choice, visit places you live to go and bridge with people who make you feel at home.

Life will become ever charming, contented, blissful and king size.

Thoughts from all!

07/11/22, 23:29 - Anuj Gupta: Thought for today!

I have been writing about various subjects. Life is versatile. So many new things happen from time to time, things change, times change, a lot changes. However, certain aspects of life remain unchanged. We talk about Values, Relations, Emotions and various other subjects, there is one topic that needs focus as it is an ever ending , everlasting and ever loving part of life for everyone. Let us talk about Friendship.

One day, I was dreaming of connecting my inner soul to the power of the Almighty. I just happened to come out of my inner self and had a look over the world integrating with the divine power of my soul. I found that the entire world is big, versatile and has so many colors. I realised that the world is colorful, life is colorful and it all depends on an individual as to how one fills life with those colors. I decided to take a long walk and analyse the different facets.

One grows up, gets into relations, progresses in life. earns money, status and migrates from one stage of life to another stage and thus the journey goes on. I somehow felt that at every stage, a green line goes along and shadows its glory over one and makes it beautiful every moment.

I retrospected to find out what  it was. After a long analysis, I found that It was FRIENDSHIP. 

I asked the Almighty as to what it meant for the humans. I was wondering as in a world of diversity, what was the need and place for this newly explored green aspect of life? 

There was silence for some time and then I could hear the voice of God.

God said, "Look My child, you are born in this world and you have a journey to carry on, accomplish various tasks every moment, every day and in every phase of life. There are moments when you tend to take a break, go back and think ............What have you been doing, what do you need to be happy, how to explore your soul and realise your power, how do you come out of your sufferings, how to fill your life with happiness, how to take the best out of life in its entirety?????"

I was lost in thoughts. I couldn't get an answer. Only thing I could think was that the Almighty should stay with me every moment, shadow me, guide me and fill me with positivity every moment!!!!!!!!

God smiled and said, "I know what you are thinking..............That is the reason I was inspired to create FRIENDSHIP. I have been with everyone at all times and I sent my message to you through my Angels whom I defined as Friends. Now it is upto you to analyze and find out who your real Friends are!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!"

I got awake and understood the gist of life. Life changed!!!

I dedicate this to this group and I am blessed and empowered in entirety. Kudos to all!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!
