30/11/22, 09:22 - Anuj Gupta: SOME SOCIAL RULES THAT MAY HELP YOU:

1. Don’t call someone more than twice continuously. If they don’t pick up your call, presume they have something important to attend to;

2. Return money that you have borrowed even before the person that borrowed you remember or ask for it. It shows your integrity and character. Same goes with umbrellas, pens and lunch boxes.

3. Never order the expensive dish on the menu when someone is giving you a lunch/dinner.

4. Don’t ask awkward questions like ‘Oh so you aren’t married yet?’ Or ‘Don’t you have kids’ or ‘Why didn’t you buy a house?’ Or why don't you buy a car? For God’s sake it isn’t your problem;

5. Always open the door for the person coming behind you. It doesn’t matter if it is a guy or a girl, senior or junior. You don’t grow small by treating someone well in public;

6. If you take a taxi with a friend and he/she pays now, try paying next time;

7. Respect different shades of opinions. Remember what's 6 to you will appear 9 to someone facing you. Besides, second opinion is good for an alternative;

8. Never interrupt people talking. Allow them to pour it out. As they say, hear them all and filter them all;

9. If you tease someone, and they don’t seem to enjoy it, stop it and never do it again. It encourages one to do more and it shows how appreciative you're;

10. Say “thank you” when someone is helping you.

11. Praise publicly. Criticize privately;

12. There’s almost never a reason to comment on someone’s weight. Just say, “You look fantastic.” If they want to talk about losing weight, they will;

13. When someone shows you a photo on their phone, don’t swipe left or right. You never know what’s next;

14. If a colleague tells you they have a doctors' appointment, don’t ask what it’s for, just say "I hope you’re okay". Don’t put them in the uncomfortable position of having to tell you their personal illness. If they want you to know, they'll do so without your inquisitiveness;

15. Treat the cleaner with the same respect as the CEO. Nobody is impressed at how rude you can treat someone below you but people will notice if you treat them with respect;

16. If a person is speaking directly to you, staring at your phone is rude;

17. Never give advice until you’re asked;

18. When meeting someone after a long time, unless they want to talk about it, don’t ask them their age and salary;

19. Mind your business unless anything involves you directly - just stay out of it;

20. Remove your sunglasses if you are talking to anyone in the street. It is a sign of respect. Moreso, eye contact is as important as your speech; and

21. Never talk about your riches in the midst of the poor. Similarly, don't talk about your children in the midst of the barren.

22. After reading a good message try to say "Thanks for the message".

APPRECIATION remains the easiest way of getting what you don't have.

04/01/23, 18:32 - Anuj Gupta: Thought for the Day!

How do we define Success?

Well, everyone has a different perception and a different definition of success.
For some people, making good money from a job or a business is a success story.
For someone, getting good marks in the exams is success.
For someone, treating the patients well and curing them is success.
For someone, leading a team to stand at the top of the race is success.
And so on...

I think, from where I would want to look at it, I would define success as a result of actions which contributed or led directly or indirectly to solve a complex problem(s) and improve someone's life.

Failures act as catalysts and at the same time as a source of information pool which apprise one to gather and analyse data to refine the actions and succeed next time!

16/01/23, 23:05 - Anuj Gupta: A violinist played for 45 minutes in the New York subway.  A handful of people stopped, a couple clapped, and the violinist raised about $30 in tips. 

No one knew this, but the violinist was Joshua Bell, one of the best musicians in the world. In that subway, Joshua played one of the most intricate pieces ever written with a violin worth 3.5 million dollars.

Two days before he played in the subway, Joshua Bell sold out a Boston theatre, and the seats averaged about $100. 

The experiment proved that the extraordinary in an ordinary environment does not shine and is so often overlooked and undervalued.

There are brilliantly talented people everywhere who aren’t receiving the recognition and reward they deserve. But once they arm themselves with value and confidence and remove themselves from an environment that isn’t serving them, they thrive and grow.  

Your gut is telling you something. Listen to it if it’s telling you where you are isn’t enough!  

Go where you are appreciated and valued. 

Know Your Worth.

01/04/23, 08:50 - Anuj Gupta: *Teacher, Trainer, Tutor, Mentor*

Teacher teaches in class, handholds the student from start of the curriculum to completion. Imparts knowledge. Teacher is the guide to venture into a new territory.

Trainer is the one who explains a subject in particular from the usage aspect in professional world. He converts the bookish content to the use in the practicality.

Tutor is the one who helps to build the knowledge from the aspect of already studied curriculum and helping to provide more clarity.

Mentor is the one above all these. He or she does not teach any curriculum. They handhold the student, walk along and mentor to learn in totality as to how to solve problems and build solutions in the subjects.

You are a MENTOR.

02/04/23, 19:20 - Anuj Gupta: Thought for this week

1. Life is full of experiences, learnings, ups and downs. Each of us strives for the best in life. 

2. However, everyone has had different paths and their own ways to do things. 

3. I have felt over the years that nobody in this World is born perfect. 

4. Success comes through a set of well defined and strategized actions. 

5. Perseverance and optimistic approach is a must in any facet of life. 

6. The question that arises is as to what is the foremost requirement as and when we undertake a challenge or an assignment or a project or a responsibility or whatever we might call, basically something that needs to get the results delivered.

7. Is this - Knowledge, Strategy, Energy, People management, Crisis management or Capability to lead?

8. I think nobody has ever had a complete answer. Gist is that as and when we move ahead, we devise our path, overcome the thresholds, break barriers and get the results.

9. One question that arises here : What is the role of a Guide? 

10. These could be parents at home, teachers in schools, professors in colleges, tutors in institutes, managers in offices etc.

11. So, in a nutshell, we need someone(s) to do the hand holding, Isn't it?

12. So, here is my analysis that I have gathered over years of learning and working.

13. We have Teachers...We were taught that teachers teach us in schools and colleges....
..................We have Tutors....We were told that tutors supplement our school or college education if that is not sufficient to understand the subjects.. 
..............We have Trainers....We were told that the trainers are the people who deliver knowledge for a particular subject(s) in the professional world...
...............We have Technologists....We have been seeing that the technologists work to make lives easier by solving complex problems ...  

14. WHOM DO WE NEED THE MOST?

?
?
?
?
?

15. I used to go around and ask people in my college days , and everyone gave different answers. Many people didn't get my question. They just ignored me 🙂 

16. Years later, I got the answer....

17. We get all these people at different stages in different forms. They all help us to learn about the world.

18. However.....the person that we NEED the most in our lives and most of the times, we donot realise the value of this person...

19. Who is this person?

20. Years of research gave me this answer!

WE NEED A MENTOR.....
 
21. How many of us actually understand what a Mentor means?

22. A mentor does not teach, does not train, does not give download of knowledge, does not develop our skills....

23. A mentor is the one who walks along, explains us how to handle problems of life, guides us to convert tasks into well defined actions, convert challenges into interesting projects, helps to convert failures into learnings and move on the path to SUCCESS!

24. Many of us might agree that Mentoring holds the key!

25. Happy Mentoring!

03/04/23, 10:41 - Anuj Gupta: 1. I am quite adapt to collecting data and doing analysis. 

2. One fine day, I decided to talk to my Subconscious and analyse various aspects of the way things go along in life.

3. We were walking beside. My subconscious asked me as to what was my concern🤔.

4. I would address the subconscious as S.

5. I said that we should talk about sufferings. 

6. S said that He didnot understand this word and wanted me to explain.

7. I said something that gives a unpleasant impact to the heart and mind is suffering.

8. S smiled. 

9. S asked me as how it affected my inner soul?

10. I said that I felt as if I was losing a lot and missing things.

11. S told me that I needed to look at it from a different angle. We suffer in life because our expectations and the resultants donot align. 

12. I was silent for a while. 

13. I asked S as to why do we expect?

14. S again got silent for a while. Then asked me if I had ever analysed as to how a plant grows. 

15. I said that we plant a seed in the soil. Then we put water in it. Then it gets sun light. Then it goes through changes of weather and it grows. Then it gives fruits etc.

16. Then S asked if this plant 🪴 expects that it gives fruits despite so many sufferings, it goes through and still it never expects that it would be watered or given care.

17. I got some clarity. I said that if the plant starts getting into expectations, nobody would get fruits and shadow.

18. S asked if this stopped, then what would happen to the World?

19. I said the entire ecosystem world get disturbed.

20. S then smiled and again asked as to what suffering meant for me now?

21. Now my thoughts were changed. 

22. I said that sufferings were my notions, the way I reacted to the actions and conveyed the resultant feelings to my soul.

23. S asked as to how I would want to change it now.

*24. I replied that I would look at these as learnings and improvise my thoughts. I was reacting earlier and I now I would act instead of reacting.*

25. S now hugged me and said that I had got the real gist now.

26. Then S asked me as to how I united my soul with the Almighty?

27. I said that God is within my soul. I just think of the unending light that comes from Him and all darkness goes away.

28. S smiled and said that now I was good to move on as I had got the key to stay contented.

29. Life is all about experiences and learnings. 

30. What we perceive could be a thought for us. However, it needs to be analysed from different angles with impact purview.

31. Do things in the spirit of Eternal love and dedicate yourself to that Super power which controls and manages the Trinity.

32. Live life to the fullest and the best. Every moment is precious, a day is too long and time is Eternal!!!

04/04/23, 10:48 - Anuj Gupta: Thought for today!

1. I was doing self introspection and retrospection.

2. I had certain thoughts accumulated in my mind. 

3. I was wondering as to what is the essence of life? What is it that is foremost important to have a contented and enriched life?

4. 
Money?
Influence?
Fame?
Power?
Prosperity?
Devotion?

5. Can money buy everything in this world. If yes, then why do  we still suffer?

6. Other factors- they compliment us but still the equation remains incomplete.

7. I agree that everyone has a different perception. What appears as M to someone, appears as W to the other. After all everyone is different😐.

8. Contentment is a state of mind. What we perceive is what we infer and inference is someone’s own intellect!

9. I think that we all have a predefined mind set which is quite judgemental and has a tendency to do the things the way we want them to be.

10. So, the points that are mentioned above are considered and assessed differently by all and it is a mix in every situation.

11. What we need to understand is as to what we want to accomplish in life, how we want to go ahead, what is our methodology to carve out our action plan, how we want to create a difference in positive aspects and how the value is generated in all facets of life?🤔

12. We all start our day with plans, make schedules, do our work and get results. 

13. Do we ever do a SWOT analysis of what all we did in  the day (Strength, Weekness, Opportunities and Threat)?

14. We follow our beliefs, we admire our principles, we strongly support our decisiveness. 

15. However, do we ever analyse the degree of contentment that we got at the closing of the day. Or we were simply counting our bank balances 😇😇

16. How did our actions and reactions make a difference. Did we create a thought for someone that we brought positivity?

17. There are lessons and teachings that we get from our Principals and Principles (try to understand these words and their gist here) and what we tend to give others to follow.

18. In reality, have we ever understood the gist of these ourselves and applied them in reality to our lives. If yes, have we measured the resultant?

19. Things need to be simplified. 

20. 1+1=2 . Why do we tend to create our own equations and complicate the thoughts?

21. Why do we tend to portray ourselves to be perfectionists when we donot have clear answers to very basis questions?

22. Contentment comes from one simple belief which is simplistic and honest way of doing things. 

23. We need to come out of our shells that we have created and hided ourselves in these.

24. We portray what we are not and what we are, we ourselves forget at times!

25. Think through and get enriched and contented!

07/04/23, 14:54 - Anuj Gupta: Thought for today!

1. I have been thinking about this subject at times and a lot of thoughts come up. 

2. We talk about being rich or poor or middle class at times. What exactly do these mean from the perspective of one's perception?

3. First of all, we need to define what it means by being rich? Is this referring to someone's bank balance, or the property that one has had or the business turnover or what is it?

4. In majority, it drills down to money. So, is money everything that one can vouch for or is this something much beyond?

5. Look, there are three entities: Necessities, Comforts and Luxuries!

6. Majority of the people around us work to fulfill their necessities. It takes years for a person to move from making 10,000 to 100,000 a month. 

7. So, if we ask a person from the lower range, they would not even bother to differentiate these three. They would have had their own ways of enjoying life.  

8. Ask a person from the higher band. They would still contemplate deciding if their daily expenses are met. Reason, higher the inflow, the more is the need to spend. 

9. A person with more money will tend to have a bigger need to save than a person with lesser money many times. 

10. So, where is the Math and how is this done?

11. So, it gets difficult to understand how we define Wealthy (state of being rich).

12. Somebody once told me. Earning is important. Spending is the requirement. However, when to spend, how much to spend and where to spend - these are very important and most of us do not have clarity on managing it. We just tend to run after the numbers.

13. Life is full of colors and experiences. 

14. Savings are earnings. Earnings need to be saved.

15. I think from where I look at it, it is more important to have a qualitative perspective on this than being quantitative.

16. Go for quality in life. Segregate the things among Good, Better and the Best. 

17. Look for the best. Do not compromise. 

18. Anything which appears costly may not be worthy every time. At the same time, something which is not expensive may not be inferior in quality. We need to have a clear thought on this.

19. We need to understand and recognize the difference between glass and diamond. Both look transparent.

20. However, glass is fragile and breaks while diamond is strong and the whole world knows its strength and the worth.

21. State of being rich or poor does not teach this difference. It is your intellect. Utilize it to the fullest and the best.

22. We do not get richer by what we have earned or saved. 

23. Rather, we become rich by virtue of how we have helped people with us to become rich. 

24. Greatness does not come by doing great things. Understand what it means. Greatness is accomplished by making the things around us great. This is the gist of life and very important to understand.

25. 
*Necessities for someone might be comforts for another person. 

*Comfort for someone might be the basic requirement for someone. 

*Something which could be a luxury for a person could be the need for another person. 

*Something which is a basic need for someone could be a luxury for another person. 

26. Read these lines again and again and understand what these mean. These define the entire life.

27. We become rich by our deeds, our acheivements, value generation and by how much we diminish the sufferings of the human mankind. 

28. To have lot of thoughts is not important. 

29. What is important is that we think through and get the value out of those thoughts and implement in life with one view - how to generate value which helps to make life easier and better for someone.

30. Define your Circle of Influence. Do we know what it means?

*Inner circle - We and our families.
*Outer circle - People around us and the whole world.

31. Need to generate value for the ecosystem. That is the core! 

32. Fill your mind with great thoughts. Have a great day!

01/05/23, 20:41 - Anuj Gupta: *Thought for today!*

1. I have had a thought about this subject of one's fitment in a system!

2. Let us get into the depths of this. I think as and when a person thinks of one's personality and traits, one thing that definitely comes in his mind as to how one fits among the people around.

3. Every individual is different - different personality, different thoughts, different qualities, different deltas, different perceptions and different goals in life. 

4. The point that I want to emphasize is that one should know about what kind of society, what kind of circle, what kind of place and various other factors ; one can fit in.

5. How is this relevant to one's success in life, one's prosperity and one's way to live a soulful, peaceful and contented life?

6. Humans are social beings. To live alone is difficult and we all need to be among people. However, everyone walks alone at some or the other time.

7. I think everyone needs to be clear about one's interests. One needs to understand what kind of people would understand one, value one and vice versa. If this is clear then the association generates value for everyone.

8. To be educated does not mean as to how qualified one is. What it means is how well one can understand the situations, the subjects and have a wise and intelligent thinking about addressing these.

9. The more experience one gains, one should learn to have a better analysis of subjects , better methodology to handle these and then yield better results.

10. However, one needs to be surrounded by people whom one understands and who understands one. 

11. Look, one doesn't buy everything which is costly and at the same time, everything which is costly may not be worth buying.

12. We can buy anything that is not costly but everything which does not have a high cost may not be worth considering too.

13. Everyone cannot be friends but at the same time, one cannot go and find friends everywhere.

14. If one keeps looking for perfect people in this world, one would be left alone. 

15. However, at the same time, one needs to have perfect people from the perspective of fitting in one's kind of ecosystem. 

16. So, one has to be selective and intelligent. Respect everyone's thoughts!

17. So what is the message? 

18. Anyone and everyone:
Realize your inner self
Understand your goals of life
Revisit your values
Respect your thoughts 
19. Then look for friends who understand you and walk along on longer paths. 

20. A mutually respectful association which generates positivity and makes life more contented and happy!

- Home to ISBT, Kashmere Gate by BluSmart or Uber. -Board Volvo bus to Manali. -Home cooked snacks at Kurukshetra when bus takes a halt. Avoid outside food in the bus journey.

*Day 2:  Sunday, June 4*

-Arrival at Manali bus stand at 10am. 
-Walk to the hotel (400 meters) and Check in.
-Breakfast at the hotel. 
-Then relax in the lawns of the resort and have leisure. Play games etc. 
-In the late afternoon, visit Van Vihar and Hadimba temple which is a 2kms trek. On the way enjoy Beas river. 

-Evening , dinner on Mall Road and then back to Hotel.

*Day 3: Monday, June 5*

-Morning leisure at the resort. 
-Breakfast at hotel. 

-Visit to Rohtang Pass by Himachal Tourism Bus. 

-Evening fun at Vashishth Kund (Hot Water Springs). 

-Enroute see Nehru Kund and Jogini waterfalls. Evening at the resort and dinner at Mall Road.

*Day 4: Tuesday, June 6*

-Visit to Solang Valley by local transport or hotel cab. 

-Full day at Solang. Snacks at Solang. 
-Late afternoon return to Manali and walk around. 

-Then return back to resort. -Dinner at Mall Road.

*Day 5: Wednesday, June 7 *
-Breakfast at the hotel. 
-Local shopping at Mall Road and lunch. 
-Board the Volvo from Manali bus stand at 4pm to Delhi. -Enroute have dinner at Bilaspur or Mandi. Or get dinner packed in Manali restaurant.

*Day 6: Thursday, June 8*

-Arrive at ISBT, Kashmere Gate. 
-Board Ola cab to reach home. 
-Lunch at home. 
-Evening walk at the garden. 

*Tour concludes.*

04/07/23, 17:21 - Anuj Gupta: Good Day All!

I would want to take this opportunity to put up my candidacy for the post of Head - Girl.

If given a chance, I would work to improve the parents teachers communication and increase transparency in the state of school affairs.

I would ensure that there are regular practices suggested to the school management which can help to increase the exposure of students to learn about the business world. 

Such activities may be regular visits to industry, read case studies and also attend lectures may be remotely or through visits of experienced professors in the school.

I would also suggest to the management to share with parents from time to time about the latest regulations and amendments made by the education ministry. 

I would form a student association where students will put up their points which need improvement and also share best practices which can lead to better results if adopted by other students.

I would also inculcate the idea of following balanced life style encompassing Yoga and enriched diet plan for the students as well as the families. 

Overall, I would try to lead by examples and help the students by generating awareness as to how to lead a healthy and prosperous life with simplicity.
08/07/23, 13:19 - Anuj Gupta: Thought of the Day!

Life gives experiences. At times in life , we come across situations which are unpredictable. We don't understand as to what to decide and what is right? One thought that comes to mind is that at times, the power of a good soul is very strong and has the ability to understand the right step to be taken and take the appropriate path. 

The biggest question that comes up is as how to understand the situation which puts one to get into a space where he loses the intellectual decision making power. What is it? Fear is the biggest factor. Messages that the brain sends us are basically according to what we are thinking and our entire system starts functioning that way. If you feel scared that something may happen to you, you immediately develop that fear and then your brain starts showing you those symptoms. Over and excessive thinking is sin.

Now what is the way to handle these?

If you do not have the capability, then listen to what the other is saying. believe him and follow. Some people are born leaders and have the capability to analyse the situation and address it. They are not scared.

You know what the gist is. We all talk about a lot of things in life. We talk of success, failures, achievements, goals and big fundamentals. How many of us make our lives simple? How many look at the reality of life . Do we have the capability to pre-sense the situations and handle them?

Those few exceptional people are the ones who have that divine power in them which connects them every time to that superpower which controls this Universe. They actually have that energy which fills their and everyone's life with positivity and life. Gist is to adore them and admire them.

Question is as to how we can become like them. My answer is we cannot. They are born like this. They did not work to make them like this. All was inherited from the Super Power. Admire them, adore them, follow them and above all, learn from their actions and try to inculcate in ourselves.
